If no effect exists, create a new one with changeAmount as value //example call: changeGlobalEffect(77, 4002, 0.005) function changeGlobalEffect(affectedCandidate, answer, changeAmount) { let found = false; // Loop through each object in the JSON array campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_global_json.forEach((item) => { // Check if the affected candidate and answer fields match the provided values if (item.fields.affected_candidate === affectedCandidate && item.fields.answer === answer) { // Update the global_multiplier item.fields.global_multiplier += changeAmount; found = true; } }); // If no matching entry was found, create a new one if (!found) { const lastEntry = campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_global_json[campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_global_json.length - 1]; const newEntry = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(lastEntry)); // Clone the last entry newEntry.pk = lastEntry.pk + 1; newEntry.fields.affected_candidate = affectedCandidate; newEntry.fields.answer = answer; newEntry.fields.global_multiplier = changeAmount; // Overwrite global_multiplier with changeAmount campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_global_json.push(newEntry); } } //change a state effect, searches for candidate and answers and state. ` } ]; function getTooltips(str) { let matches = []; tooltipList.forEach((tooltip, index) => { // Adjust the regex to match searchString with optional punctuation afterward let regex = new RegExp(`\\b${tooltip.searchString}\\b[.,;!?]?`, 'g'); let match = regex.exec(str); if (match !== null) { // Only push the first match found for this tooltip matches.push({ start: match.index, end: match.index + match[0].length, tooltipIndex: index }); } }); matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || (b.end - b.start) - (a.end - a.start)); // Filter out overlaps for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1; ) { if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) { matches.splice(i + 1, 1); // Remove the next match since it overlaps } else { i++; // Move to the next match } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; matches.forEach(match => { const tooltip = tooltipList[match.tooltipIndex]; result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.start); // Create the Wikipedia-style tooltip structure let tooltipContent = `

${tooltip.searchString}

`; // Check if the explanationText contains an image if (tooltip.explanationText.includes(''); tooltipContent += `${imagePart}/>`; tooltipContent += `

${textPart.trim()}

`; } else { // If no image, just add the explanation text as a paragraph tooltipContent += `

${tooltip.explanationText}

`; } result += `${tooltip.searchString}${tooltipContent}`; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); // Add the remainder of the original string return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]); } else if (typeof obj[key] === 'object') { applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]); // Recursive call } } } function boldBudgetChanges(str) { const budgetChangeRegex = /([+-]\d+ Budget)/g; // Matches patterns like (+2 Budget), (-1 Budget), etc. let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; // Find all matches of budget change patterns const matches = [...str.matchAll(budgetChangeRegex)]; matches.forEach(match => { result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.index); // Add text before the match result += `${match[0]}`; // Wrap the match in bold tags lastIndex = match.index + match[0].length; // Update the lastIndex }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); // Add the remainder of the original string return result; } function applyBoldToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = boldBudgetChanges(obj[key]); } else if (typeof obj[key] === 'object') { applyBoldToObject(obj[key]); // Recursive call for nested objects } } } applyBoldToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answers_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json);
